update_fields[\"deleted_by\"] = deleted_by\n\n        return self.update(**update_fields)\n\n    soft_delete.alters_data = True\n\n    def restore(self) -> int:\n        \"\"\"\n        Restore soft-deleted records in the queryset.\n\n        Marks records as not deleted by setting is_deleted=False and clearing\n        the deletion timestamp and deleted_by fields.\n\n        Returns:\n            The number of records restored.\n\n        Raises:\n            TypeError: If the queryset has been sliced or if values/values_list\n                      has been called.\n\n        Example:\n self.query.is_sliced:\n            raise TypeError(\"Cannot restore a query once a slice has been taken.\")\n        if self.query.distinct_fields:\n            raise TypeError(\"Cannot call restore() The number of records restored.\n\n        Example:\n            # Restore users with IDs 1, 2, and 3\n            User.objects.restore_by_ids([1, 2, 3])\n        \"\"\"\n        return
